 The validity of the old card was till December 31, 2018 only

 The process of using atms has also changed since the introduction of new chip cards
 agar aapane haal hi main ATM kaa istemaal kiya hoga to aapako ye jaankaree hogi bhi
 You must have noticed that during ATM usage nowadays, you have to keep the card attached to the ATM during the whole process

 'we have upgraded the security features on our atms and recyclers
